              ,T.CREATION_DATE
              ,CASE T2.BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END BIN_STATUS
              ,CASE T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN '_' THEN '在库' WHEN 'O' THEN '预约出库' WHEN 'I' THEN '预约入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '其他' END BIN_BIZ_STATUS
              ,T.PALLET_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NAME
              ,T1.PRODUCT_GUID
              ,T1.PRODUCT_DATE
              ,T1.PRODUCT_QTY
              ,T1.MAIN_UNIT
         FROM WBS_BIN T
         LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
         LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2 ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1
参数：
@param0=2018/1/25 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/26 0:00:00

2019-01-26 08:27:51,958 [8] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-26 09:12:56,260 [27] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.CrnService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.CrnService.GetCrnDataTable
 
      SELECT T.CRN_FORK_NO,T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE,T1.*,
             CASE T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_FORK_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_IN_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_IN_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_OUT_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_OUT_ENABLE_DESC
        FROM PSB_CRN_FORK T
        JOIN PSB_CRN T1 
          ON T1.CRN_NO = T.CRN_NO

2019-01-26 09:14:49,227 [15] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@InOutBinHistory
SELECT T.BIN_GUID,
        T.BIN_NO,
        CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库'
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
        END IO_TYPE,
        T.CREATION_DATE,
        T.PALLET_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NO,T2.MATER_NO) MATER_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T2.MATER_NAME) MATER_NAME,
        CASE WHEN T.FINISH_FLAG IS NULL OR T.FINISH_FLAG = '_' THEN '正常'
        ELSE T.FINISH_FLAG END FINISH_FLAG,
        CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN ISNULL(T3.SLOC_NO,T4.SLOC_NO)
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN ISNULL(T3.ELOC_NO,T4.ELOC_NO) 
        END LOC_NO,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_NO,T4.TASK_NO) TASK_NO,
        ISNULL(T3.CREATION_DATE,T4.CREATION_DATE) CREATE_TASK_DATE,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T4.TASK_EXEC_START_DT) TASK_EXEC_START_DT,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,T4.TASK_EXEC_END_DT) TASK_EXEC_END_DT
        FROM Z50_WBS_BIN T
        LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T2 ON T2.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK T3 ON T3.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK T4 ON T4.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1
参数：
@param0=2019/1/21 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/26 0:00:00

SELECT T.BIN_NO
              ,T.CREATION_DATE
              ,CASE T2.BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END BIN_STATUS
              ,CASE T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN '_' THEN '在库' WHEN 'O' THEN '预约出库' WHEN 'I' THEN '预约入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '其他' END BIN_BIZ_STATUS
              ,T.PALLET_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NAME
              ,T1.PRODUCT_GUID
              ,T1.PRODUCT_DATE
              ,T1.PRODUCT_QTY
              ,T1.MAIN_UNIT
         FROM WBS_BIN T
         LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
         LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2 ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1

@param0=2018/1/25 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/26 0:00:00

2019-01-26 10:03:18,760 [51] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService.GetBinCheckDataInfo
SELECT B.PACKAGE_GUID,B.BIN_NO,B.CREATION_DATE,D.MATER_NO,D.MATER_NAME,D.PALLET_NO,D.BATCH_NO,D.PRODUCT_QTY,D.PRODUCT_DATE,P.MEMO,
	      (CASE WHEN D.CHECK_STATUS=0 THEN　'待检'　WHEN　D.CHECK_STATUS=1 THEN '合格' ELSE '不合格'  END) CHECK_STATUS
        FROM WBS_PACKAGE_DATA D inner join WBS_BIN B on B.PACKAGE_GUID=D.PACKAGE_GUID 
		    LEFT JOIN PSB_PRODUCT P ON P.PRODUCT_GUID=D.PRODUCT_GUID
		    WHERE D.MATER_NO <> 'BPALLET'
        
        ORDER BY B.creation_date

2019-01-26 11:46:34,773 [10] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-26 14:12:46,529 [24] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@InOutBinHistory
SELECT T.BIN_GUID,
        T.BIN_NO,
        CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库'
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
        END IO_TYPE,
        T.CREATION_DATE,
        T.PALLET_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NO,T2.MATER_NO) MATER_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T2.MATER_NAME) MATER_NAME,
        CASE WHEN T.FINISH_FLAG IS NULL OR T.FINISH_FLAG = '_' THEN '正常'
        ELSE T.FINISH_FLAG END FINISH_FLAG,
        CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN ISNULL(T3.SLOC_NO,T4.SLOC_NO)
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN ISNULL(T3.ELOC_NO,T4.ELOC_NO) 
        END LOC_NO,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_NO,T4.TASK_NO) TASK_NO,
        ISNULL(T3.CREATION_DATE,T4.CREATION_DATE) CREATE_TASK_DATE,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T4.TASK_EXEC_START_DT) TASK_EXEC_START_DT,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,T4.TASK_EXEC_END_DT) TASK_EXEC_END_DT
        FROM Z50_WBS_BIN T
        LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T2 ON T2.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK T3 ON T3.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK T4 ON T4.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1
参数：
@param0=2019/1/21 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/26 0:00:00
